001306cls-8
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="cls-8" obligation="normative">
<title>ModSpec Requirements Class: Core</title>
<p id="_3939304b-c9fa-6f40-e291-a078e95e1bc0">This clause specifies the requirements and recommendations for the content and structure of a modular standard.
This collection of requirements, recommendations, and permissions are also known as the <tt>core</tt> of the ModSpec.
All the requirements specified in this ModSpec core comprise the ModSpec Core Requirements Class.</p>

001667req_​imported-requirements-class
Requirement /req/​core/imported-requirements-class has no corresponding Conformance test

<requirement id="req_imported-requirements-class" model="ogc"> <identifier>/req/core/imported-requirements-class</identifier> <component class="part"> <p id="_430d695c-ea39-568e-128d-58ea9ce6a0c6">If a requirements class is imported from another standard for use within a standard conformant to the ModSpec, and if any imported requirement is “optional,” then that requirement SHALL be factored out as a separate requirements class in the profile of that imported standard used in the conformant standard.</p>
</component> <component class="part"> <p id="_6bb66af3-3aee-8db4-cf4a-dc1d935d9e2b">Each such used requirements class SHALL be a conformance class of the source standard or a combination of conformance classes of the source standard or standards.</p>
</component>
</requirement>

001702req_req-in-only-one-req-class

</component> <component class="part"> <p id="_51923160-b936-2529-c359-6f35bcf86e80">Inclusion of any requirement in a requirements class by a conformance class SHALL imply inclusion of all requirements in its class (as a dependency).</p>
</component>
</requirement>
2



001731req_co-dependent-requirements
